The instruction asks to "Convert the following date from the Gregorian calendar to the Julian calendar," but Output (b) assumes a conversion that is generally accurate for the period before 1582. The actual conversion from the Gregorian to Julian calendar for the year 2020 is more complex due to the different leap year rules between the two calendars. In 2020, the Julian calendar was 13 days behind the Gregorian calendar, making November 29, 2020 (Gregorian), equivalent to November 16, 2020 (Julian), as Output (b) states.  Output (a), while not directly providing the Julian date, indirectly confirms the conversion method by mentioning the 13-day difference, which is correct for the year 2020.
